            <h1>Is this what Australia is coming to? Man fights $330 fine in court after seven police cars were sent to a quiet park to catch cyclists without a helmet</h1>      
      <ul class="mol-bullets-with-font"><li class="class"><b>Seven cars were in Centennial Park in Sydney on Saturday at a cyclists' protest</b></li><li class="class"><b>New laws by NSW government last year introduced $330 fines for no helmets</b></li><li class="class"><b>Fines for several riders led police to be slammed as enforcing 'nanny state' rules</b></li><li class="class"><b>Chris Standen had his case and fine thrown out of court on Monday in Sydney</b></li></ul><p class="author-section byline-plain">By

<a href="/home/search.html?s=&amp;authornamef=Matt+Leclere+For+Daily+Mail+Australia" class="author" rel="nofollow">Matt Leclere For Daily Mail Australia</a>


</p><p class="byline-section"><span class="article-timestamp article-timestamp-published">

</p><div itemprop="articleBody"><p class="mol-para-with-font">Seven police cars were sent to  catch cyclists riding around a quiet park without helmets as they patrolled the peaceful protest.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Officers told cyclists in Sydney's Centennial Park on Saturday they 'would enforce the law' as riders protested against Australia's compulsory helmet laws.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">But the approach has led to a fierce backlash from cycling groups, causing some to brand Sydney as the 'least friendly cycling city in the developed world'.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font"><span class="mol-style-bold">Scroll down for video</span></p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <div class="image-wrap">

</div><p class="mol-para-with-font">One group called the new fines 'trivial offences' and groups around Australia took to the saddle to protest.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Chris Standen had his case thrown out of court on Monday despite pleading guilty to riding without a helmet, court documents seen by Daily Mail Australia revealed.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">But the charges were dismissed by the magistrateat the Downing Centre in Sydney's CBD.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">'My $330 fine for riding a bicycle slowly and carefully while wearing a sunhat was dismissed in court this morning,' he tweeted.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">'Trivial offence, no objective risk, good character etc. What a waste of police/court time (and mine).'</p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <div class="image-wrap">
    <img id="i-67d9512f6f1873ec"
         src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/03/19/06/4A55664000000578-5517259-image-a-22_1521441460721.jpg"
         height="357" width="634" alt="Groups said cases currently before the courts was a reason for the protests held throughout Australia" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
  </div>

  <noscript>

    <img id="i-67d9512f6f1873ec" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/03/19/06/4A55664000000578-5517259-image-a-22_1521441460721.jpg" height="357" width="634" alt="Groups said cases currently before the courts was a reason for the protests held throughout Australia" class="blkBorder img-share"/>

  </noscript>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">Groups said cases currently before the courts was a reason for the protests held throughout Australia</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">He described the court case on Monday as a 'waste of time' after the charges were dropped and said it was an 'only in Australia' example.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Daily Mail Australia understands Mr Standen was wearing a sunhat and carrying a doctor's letter 'supporting his choice' when he was pulled over and fined.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">It is understood the case was unrelated and happened before the protest ride at the weekend.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Groups said cases currently before the courts was a reason for the protests held throughout Australia - including in Melbourne, Adelaide and Brisbane.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Mr Standen, who attended the ride on Saturday. slammed the 'nanny state' approach by NSW Police.</p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <div class="image-wrap">
    <img id="i-d38c00f41b09b236"
         src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/03/19/06/4A55663700000578-5517259-image-a-23_1521441465676.jpg"
         height="357" width="634" alt="The incident at the park on Saturday was also described as a PR disaster for NSW Police" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
  </div>

  <noscript>

    <img id="i-d38c00f41b09b236" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/03/19/06/4A55663700000578-5517259-image-a-23_1521441465676.jpg" height="357" width="634" alt="The incident at the park on Saturday was also described as a PR disaster for NSW Police" class="blkBorder img-share"/>

  </noscript>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">The incident at the park on Saturday was also described as a PR disaster for NSW Police</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">Riders said they felt targeted by the officers who were deployed for around two hours.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Kathy Francis, the secretary of campaign group Freestyle Cyclists, said NSW Police had taken a 'punitive approach to cyclists', she told Daily Mail Australia</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">'It is so disappointing that the NSW Police were unable to handle this situation in a more constructive way,' she added.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">'The example from the other States and even from NSW in a previous protest, demonstrates that good policing can facilitate safe community protest in a way that builds good relations between the police and the public.'</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The incident at the park on Saturday was also described as a public relations disaster for the force.</p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <div class="image-wrap">
    <img id="i-b7905f44806ce76"
         src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/03/19/06/4A55663B00000578-5517259-image-a-24_1521441470074.jpg"
         height="357" width="634" alt="One woman was issued with an on-the-spot fine for riding without a helmet but protested the charge with an officer" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
  </div>

  <noscript>

    <img id="i-b7905f44806ce76" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/03/19/06/4A55663B00000578-5517259-image-a-24_1521441470074.jpg" height="357" width="634" alt="One woman was issued with an on-the-spot fine for riding without a helmet but protested the charge with an officer" class="blkBorder img-share"/>

  </noscript>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">One woman was issued with an on-the-spot fine for riding without a helmet but protested the charge with an officer</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">Cyclists in New South Wales are now subjected to fines of $330 for riding without a helmet after new rules were introduced by roads minister Duncan Gray last year.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">They argue cycling should be encouraged as congestion increases but the ride challenged the threats of high fines 'for something that is considered normal and is having the opposite effect'.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The protest was also held in Melbourne, Adelaide and Brisbane but faced controversy in Sydney.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Ms Francis added: 'NSW has fewer bike riders and a poorer safety record than the rest of the country and internationally is gaining a reputation as the least friendly cycling city in the developed world.'</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Footage shared by the Freestyle Cyclists page showed an officer telling cyclists that they would enforce the law.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Later in the clip, a woman is pulled over by an officer and is told she would be receiving a penalty notice.</p><div class="artSplitter mol-img-group">    <div class="mol-img">  <div class="image-wrap">
    <img id="i-162a55eba800ed99"
         src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/03/19/06/4A55574C00000578-5517259-image-a-25_1521441498724.jpg"
         height="673" width="634" alt="Chris Standen was due in court anyway on Monday but had his case thrown out despite pleading guilty" class="blkBorder img-share"/>
  </div>

  <noscript>

    <img id="i-162a55eba800ed99" src="http://i.dailymail.co.uk/i/newpix/2018/03/19/06/4A55574C00000578-5517259-image-a-25_1521441498724.jpg" height="673" width="634" alt="Chris Standen was due in court anyway on Monday but had his case thrown out despite pleading guilty" class="blkBorder img-share"/>

  </noscript>
</div>    <p class="imageCaption">Chris Standen was due in court anyway on Monday but had his case thrown out despite pleading guilty</p></div><p class="mol-para-with-font">The woman responds saying the new laws had made cycling dangerous because drivers no longer 'share the roads'.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">She also criticises the police for showing a 'lack of discretion'.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Rule 256 of the new cycling rules states arider must wear an Australian Standard approved bicycle helmet, securely fitted and fastened on the riders head.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">The fine for not complying increased from $71 to $319 when it was introduced.</p><p class="mol-para-with-font">Daily Mail Australia has approached NSW Police for comment.</p></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    DM.later('bundle', function(){
        var n = 0;
        var taboola_every_n = 10;
        var taboola_counter = 0;

        var addTaboola = function (node){
            var id = "taboola-stream-thumbnails-" + (++n);
            var taboola_node = '<div id="' + id + '" style="min-height: 280px;"></div>';
            $(node).before(taboola_node);

            window._taboola = window._taboola || [];
            _taboola.push({
                mode: 'thumbnails-b',
                container: id,
                placement: "Stream Thumbnails " + n,
                target_type: 'mix'
            });
        };

        DM.has('infinite-list', 'InfiniteList', {
url: '/api/infinite-list.html?channelShortName=news&pageSize=10',
            total: 24.0,
            from: 0,
            onAfterAppend: function (container){
                var items = $(container).children('div');
                if(!taboola_every_n){
                    return;
                }

                items.each(function (){
                    if (taboola_counter == 0){
                        addTaboola(this);
                        taboola_counter = taboola_every_n - 1;
                    }
                    else {
                        taboola_counter--;
                    }
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>
